Attached is the installation guide. It has been reviewed by Ari, Marc
and Sam. I consider this 60% complete. =20

Reason for 60%

*       Marc continues to make changes to the installation process=20

*       We need information about installing on multiple servers

*       General system requirements and sizing are not yet available

*       As Ari goes to more demos, he may find planning issues that can
be added

*       When I am able to install the system, I will probably come
across issues or questions to things I didn't think to ask about

*       Migration Wizard, I need to be able to run it to capture the
screen shots

=20

Kevin, I am sending it to you for your general review whenever you have
time.

=20

Matt, I am sending it to you to use in QA.  Please use the guide when
you do installations or run the migration wizard and send me your
feedback.  When you use the document during installation, let me know if
there are any questions that were not answers, steps incorrectly
described, etc.  When do you think QA will be focusing on installation
or the Migration Wizard operation?  Can I have feedback by June 20 or do
you think you will need more time? =20

=20

=20

=20

Candace

=20

=20
